< review>
Adopted 2 very healthy kittens who easily adapted to our family.  After the first evening they had explored their environment and were ready to be sociable.   Staff had carefully matched our family to ready cats, but that the cats adapted so easily is a testimonial to their care in the humane society.  Not fearful at all.  Coupons in the adoption packet eased the set up costs.  Wonderful place and volunteers.< /review>

It was a great experience.  I changed my pets name from Narcissus to Mitry, short for Dimitri Shostakovich.  I name my cats for composers.

Usually my cats sleep at the foot of my bed, but I think the kitten is afraid of my other cat, so I think he sleeps in the bathroom.

The people at Valley Humane Society were more than helpful.  They were great!

A totally excellent experience!!!

Ruth Ungar</Review>

< Text>
My boyfriend and I came for a romantic Valentines day weekend. My first time at Embassy suites. Beautiful hotel. We live in Sacramento.

Hungry after our 5pm check we were presented with a beautiful romantic Valentines day menu, we ordered (Entrees at $25.99). What we received was unacceptable for the price and hotel.

The shrimp Alfredo was watered down, with 4 shrimps, (no bread, salad included/boxed mac n cheese is better). The beef tip risotto was horrible, the meat smelled bad and the risotto was mush. The "woodfire pizza" was disappointing, cheese was not cooked through.

I had no choice but to call the manager who did apologize and comped the meal, so I'm thankful for the understanding. We are here for 2 more days, so we will go out and eat instead of room service.<//Text>

< Review>
9/3/14

I enjoyed our stay at the Embassy Suites for a convention, but was a little disappointed with their only food option inside the hotel.  There are places to eat not far away in Old Sac (walking distance) and I'd definitely pick one of them over the hotel's food.

I had an over-priced wedge salad for lunch with a group of friends one afternoon (they actually bought my lunch, so that was super nice, since I didn't think the food was a good value).  Another woman had the same salad with a steak add-on and the meat looked really good, but I was still surprised at the price of the small salad, with or without meat.

The coolest thing about the restaurant area of the hotel is their outdoor seating.  They have live music and it's a pretty view of the river and Tower Bridge.  A full-bar is also in the restaurant area, but the hotel has a daily complimentary reception hour with free drinks, so we didn't have any reason to hit up the bar.

Breakfast at the Bistro was also just so-so.  My omelet was a little over-cooked, and the potatoes were terrible.  (Again, breakfast was free, so it's hard to complain)... plus, they had yogurt, cereal, juice, and other options that are hard to mess up.

A place as nice as this Embassy Suites should really step up the value and quality of the food associated with their hotel.<//Review>

<Pictures>None< /Pictures><date>1443191901413</date>< review>
In looking for a CA dealer to handle a transfer from out of CA state, was told by Gun Vault staffer that all guns shipping from another state to CA had to be sent by an FFL. (Later learned that this is BS, it is only the gun shop's policy, not CA law.) So, had my local dealer contact Gun Vault to line up shipment, only to learn that dealers shipping to CA must go through a process with CA state to acquire approval to ship a gun into the state, something my local dealer was not especially interested in doing on a one-off shipment. This was not mentioned in my earlier call with Gun Vault during which I was led to believe that simple submission of FFL was all that was needed. Wasted my time, and that of my local dealer. After researching I learned that person-to-CA FFL does NOT require the CA document/approval (explicitly stated on CA Attorney General's website). No thanks whatsoever to Gun Vault, I was able to lawfully ship as an individual to a more cooperative/less deceitful FFL in CA to successfully complete the transfer. I am aware that many CA dealers decline to handle shipments from individuals due to the CA hassles, and that is fine, but Gun Vault was dishonest in representing FFL-to-FFL as the only lawful way to handle a transfer, and further, not being up front with me re the administrative hoop-jumping required. Certainly could have been more helpful. Bottom line: I do not trust these guys and recommend that others tread carefully in considering doing business with them.<//review>

<user>101875998493251463525<//user>< username>
Catherine A. Montgomery<//username>
<date>1559082304568< /date>< Rate>

< Review>
In the centre of the Sunset Marquis hotel, surrounded by beautiful lush greenery, tricking fountain facing the patio, and a nice cabana with view of the lounge and a zen trickling fountain you will find this hidden gem.

The decor of this restaurant is quite simple: blue table cloths, fresh orchid flowers near hostess desk, an etched glass case of various libations. But the best decor here is the black and white photographs of the legends who have dined or stayed here: Robert Downey Jr, Nicole Kidman, Brad Pitt (and more). My favorite photo was a black and white of Mick Jagger on the beach from 1969 that faced the small cocktail area.

As I arrived around mid afternoon, it was lunch. The lunch menu is very simple: salads, a variety of sandwiches and several pasta and meat main dishes. All very healthy choices, served well with my choice of the day: Prosseco.

It was very relaxing and perfect quiet afternoon. The service is excellent, and the food filling. I quite enjoyed this little afternoon getaway, and I look forward to dining here again on my next visit.<//Review>

Braised Pork Belly - A little bit fattening, lots of fat but delicious. Wish there is more than one piece. $15!!

Lamb Meatballs - Tomato, cumin, pine nuts, ricotta salata. The best lamb meatballs I have ever tasted. Good portion for small plate. Very flavorful and lots of ingredient inside the meatballs. Will definitely order again.
